GT Equivalence Verification (CRK33)
============================================================
GT: -c0*sqrt(A) - c1*A**c2 + c3*_t*sin(log(A + c4))
Candidate formulas: 72

GT (fixed function of **A** only; no dependence on **t**):
\[
f(A)= -0.11846873325639269\,\sqrt{A}\;-\;0.11846873325639269\,A^2\;+\;0.84638280991099803\,\sin(\log(A+1)).
\]
Key structural facts:
- Contains a **\(\sqrt{A}\)** term (non-polynomial power \(A^{1/2}\)) with nonzero coefficient.
- Contains an **\(A^2\)** term with nonzero coefficient.
- Contains **\(\sin(\log(A+1))\)** with nonzero coefficient.
- **No \(t\)** dependence at all.

Now check each candidate: can we choose its free constants to equal this for **all** \(A,t\)?

1) \(A c0/(A c1+c2)^2 + c3\log(Ac4+1)+c5 + c6\log(c7 e^{Ac8}+1)\).  
Has only rational-in-\(A\), logs, and log(1+exp(linear)). No \(\sqrt{A}\) and no \(\sin(\log(\cdot))\). Cannot match.  

2) \(c0 + c1 e^{Ac2} + c3\log(Ac4+1) + c5\sin(c6\log(c7|A|+1)+c8)\).  
Can create a sine-of-log term, but also has \(\log(\cdot)\) (not inside sine) and/or an exponential unless coefficients set to 0. Even if set exp and log terms to 0, remaining form is constant + sine(log(affine in |A|)). Still cannot produce the required \(-k\sqrt{A}-kA^2\) polynomial/power terms. No \(\sqrt{A}\) or \(A^2\) outside sine.  

3) \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + A^{c2}c3/(A^{c2}+c4) + c5 e^{Ac6} + c7\).  
Has polynomial + saturating rational + exponential. No \(\sqrt{A}\) term and no \(\sin(\log(A+1))\).  

4) \(A^4c0 + A^2c1 + Ac2 + c3 + c4\sin(c5\log(c6 e^{c7|A|}+1)+c8)\).  
Has \(A^2\) possible, and a sine-of-log-of-(1+exp(|A|)) which is not \(\sin(\log(A+1))\). Also no \(\sqrt{A}\) term.  

5) \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + A^{c2}c3 + c4 + c5 e^{c6 t}\log(c7|A|+1)\).  
Contains explicit \(t\) unless \(c5=0\). If \(c5=0\), becomes polynomial/power only; still no sine(log) term. Also \(\sqrt{A}\) could be made by setting \(c2=1/2\), but then you still lack the sine(log(A+1)) term.  

6) \(c0 + c1 e^{Ac2} + c3\log(Ac4+1) + c5\log(c6 e^{Ac7}+1)\).  
No sine term and no \(\sqrt{A}\).  

7) \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2 e^{Ac3} + c4 + c5\sin(c6\log(c7 e^{c8|A|}+1)+c9)\).  
Can include \(A^2\) and a sine-of-log-of-(1+exp(|A|)), but not \(\sin(\log(A+1))\). No \(\sqrt{A}\) term.  

8) \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2 e^{Ac3} + c4 + c5\log(c6 e^{Ac7}+1)\).  
No sine and no \(\sqrt{A}\).  

9) \(Ac0 + A^{c1}c2 + A^{c3}c4/(A^{c3}+c5) + c6\).  
Can make \(A^{c1}\) be \(\sqrt{A}\) and also include an \(A\) term, but there is no sine(log) term, and no clean independent \(A^2\) unless you set \(c1=2\) (then you lose \(\sqrt{A}\)). Only one free power term \(A^{c1}\), so cannot simultaneously produce both \(\sqrt{A}\) and \(A^2\).  

10) \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + A c2/(Ac3+c4) + c5 + c6\log(Ac7+1) + c8/(Ac3+c4)\).  
Has \(A^2\) and log, but no sine(log) and no \(\sqrt{A}\).  

11) \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2 + c3\sin(c4\log(c5|A c6|+1)+c7)\).  
Has \(A^2\) and sine(log(affine in |A|)). But no \(\sqrt{A}\) term. Also the sine argument can be made \(\log(A+1)\) only if you can remove Abs and scaling exactly for all real A; Abs prevents equality on negative A, and even restricting to \(A\ge 0\), you still cannot generate \(-k\sqrt{A}\).  

12) \(c0 + c1\sin(Ac2+c3) + c4 e^{Ac5} + c6 \frac{\max(0,A)^{c7}}{c8+\max(0,A)^{c7}}\).  
No sine(log) and no \(\sqrt{A}\) term; also piecewise max.  

13) \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2 + c3\sin(c4\log(c5 e^{Ac6}+1)+c7)\).  
Sine of log(1+exp(linear A)), not sine(log(A+1)). No \(\sqrt{A}\).  

14) \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2 e^{Ac3} + c4 + c5\log(c6 e^{Ac7+c8 t}+1)\).  
Has explicit \(t\) unless \(c5=0\) or \(c8=0\) and still log(1+exp(linear)) not needed. No sine(log) and no \(\sqrt{A}\).  

15) \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2 + c3\log(Ac4+1) + c5\log(Ac6+1)/A\).  
No sine(log) and no \(\sqrt{A}\).  

16) \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + c2 + c3\log(Ac4+1) + c5\exp(c6\sin(c7\log(c8|A|+1)+c9))\).  
No way to get a plain \(\sin(\log(A+1))\) term (it’s inside an exp), and still no \(\sqrt{A}\).

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK33)
============================================================
GT: -c0*sqrt(A) - c1*A**c2 + c3*_t*sin(log(A + c4))
Candidates evaluated: 72
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.11847*sqrt(A) - 0.11847*A^2 + 0.84638*sin(log(A + 1))`

The GT has three basis functions:
1. `sqrt(A)` (i.e., `A^(1/2)`)
2. `A^2`
3. `sin(log(A + 1))`

Note: `_t` is a fixed constant (7.14436), so `c3*_t = 0.11847 * 7.14436 ≈ 0.84638`.

Let me check each candidate for the presence of these three basis functions.

**Key observations:** The GT requires `sqrt(A)`, `A^2`, and `sin(log(A+1))`. Any candidate must be able to produce all three of these terms (or equivalent).

Let me systematically go through candidates:

**Candidate 1:** `A*c0/(A*c1+c2)^2 + c3*log(A*c4+1) + c5 + c6*log(c7*exp(A*c8)+1)`
- Has rational function, log terms. No `sqrt(A)`, no `sin(log(...))`. No match.

**Candidate 2:** `c0 + c1*exp(A*c2) + c3*log(A*c4+1) + c5*sin(c6*log(c7*Abs(A)+1) + c8)`
- Has `sin(log(...))` term. But has `exp(A*c2)` and `log(A*c4+1)` instead of `sqrt(A)` and `A^2`. Setting c1=0 removes exp, but then we need `sqrt(A)` and `A^2` from remaining terms. We only have `c3*log(A*c4+1)` and a constant. Can't produce `sqrt(A)` or `A^2`. No match.

**Candidate 3:** `A^2*c0 + A*c1 + A^c2*c3/(A^c2+c4) + c5*exp(A*c6) + c7`
- Has `A^2`. Could set c2=0.5 for `sqrt(A)` term, but `A^0.5*c3/(A^0.5+c4)` is not `sqrt(A)`. No `sin(log(...))`. No match.

**Candidate 4:** `A^4*c0 + A^2*c1 + A*c2 + c3 + c4*sin(c5*log(c6*exp(c7*Abs(A))+1) + c8)`
- Has `sin(log(c6*exp(c7*|A|)+1))`. For A≥0, `|A|=A`. If c7→0, then `c6*exp(0)+1 = c6+1`, constant. That doesn't help. If c6=0, `sin(c5*log(1)+c8) = sin(c8)`, constant. Can't get `sin(log(A+1))` from `sin(log(c6*exp(c7*A)+1))`. No `sqrt(A)`. No match.

**Candidate 5:** `A^2*c0 + A*c1 + A^c2*c3 + c4 + c5*exp(c6*t)*log(c7*Abs(A)+1)`
- Has `A^2`, `A^c2` (could be `sqrt(A)` with c2=0.5). But has `log(|A|+1)` instead of `sin(log(A+1))`. Since t is a variable, `exp(c6*t)` makes this t-dependent (can't set c6=0 and still have the log term contribute meaningfully, but even with c6=0, we get `c5*log(...)` which is log, not sin(log)). No match.

**Candidate 6:** `c0 + c1*exp(A*c2) + c3*log(A*c4+1) + c5*log(c6*exp(A*c7)+1)`
- No `sqrt(A)`, no `A^2`, no `sin(log(...))`. No match.

**Candidate 7:** `A^2*c0 + A*c1 + c2*exp(A*c3) + c4 + c5*sin(c6*log(c7*exp(c8*Abs(A))+1) + c9)`
- Has `A^2`. Set c2=0 to remove exp. Need `sqrt(A)` from remaining: only `A*c1`, can't produce `sqrt(A)`. No match.

**Candidate 8:** Similar to 7 but with log instead of sin. No `sin(log(...))`, no `sqrt(A)`. No match.

**Candidate 9:** `A*c0 + A^c1*c2 + A^c3*c4/(A^c3+c5) + c6`
- No `sin(log(...))`. No match.

**Candidate 10:** `A^2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2/(A*c3+c4) + c5 + c6*log(A*c7+1) + c8/(A*c3+c4)`
- No `sin(log(...))`, no `sqrt(A)`. No match.

**Candidate 11:** `A^2*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*sin(c4*log(c5*Abs(A*c6)+1) + c7)`
- Has `A^2` and `sin(log(...))`. For A≥0: `sin(c4*log(c5*c6*A+1)+c7)`. Set c4=1, c5*c6=1, c7=0: `sin(log(A+1))`. ✓
- But needs `sqrt(A)`. Only has `A*c1`. Can't produce `sqrt(A)` from `A*c1`. No match.

**Candidate 12:** `c0 + c1*sin(A*c2+c3) + c4*exp(A*c5) + c6*Max(0,A)^c7/(c8+Max(0,A)^c7)`
- Has `sin(A*c2+c3)` not `sin(log(A+1))`. No match.

**Candidate 13:** `A^2*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*sin(c4*log(c5*exp(A*c6)+1) + c7)`
- `sin(c4*log(c5*exp(A*c6)+1)+c7)`. If c6→0: `sin(c4*log(c5+1)+c7)` = constant. Can't get `sin(log(A+1))` from this form since the argument of exp is linear in A, not log(A+1). No `sqrt(A)`. No match.

**Candidate 14:** Has `log(c6*exp(A*c7+c8*t)+1)` - t-dependent and no `sin(log(...))`. No match.

**Candidate 15:** `A^2*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*log(A*c4+1) + c5*log(A*c6+1)/A`
- No `sin(log(...))`, no `sqrt(A)`. No match.

**Candidate 16:** `A^2*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*log(A*c4+1) + c5*exp(c6*sin(c7*log(c8*Abs(A)+1)+c9))`
- Has `exp(c6*sin(log(...)))` not `sin(log(...))`. These are different functions. No match.

**Candidate 17:** Has `exp(c6*sin(...))` and t-dependence. No match.

**Candidate 18:** `A^2*c0 + A*c1 + A^c2*c3 + c4 + c5*sin(c6*log(c7*exp(c8*Abs(A))+1) + c9)`
- Has `A^2`, `A^c2` (set c2=0.5 for `sqrt(A)`). ✓
- `sin(c6*log(c7*exp(c8*|A|)+1)+c9)`: For A≥0, this is `sin(c6*log(c7*exp(c8*A)+1)+c9)`. Can this equal `sin(log(A+1))`? We need `c7*exp(c8*A)+1 = (A+1)^{1/c6}` with c9=0. But `c7*exp(c8*A)+1` is exponential in A while `(A+1)^{1/c6}` is polynomial. These can't be equal for all A. No match.

**Candidate 19-68:** Let me focus on candidates that have both `A^c` (for sqrt) and `sin(log(...))`.

**Candidate 38:** `A^c0*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(A*c4) + c5*cos(A*c6+c7)`
- `A^c0` with c0=0.5 gives `sqrt(A)`. But no `A^2` (unless from exp, which can't exactly give A^2). `cos(A*c6+c7)` ≠ `sin(log(A+1))`. No match.

**Candidate 50:** `c0 + c1*sin(A*c2+c3) + c4*exp(A*c5) + c6*Max(0,A)^c7`
- `Max(0,A)^c7` for A≥0 is `A^c7`. Set c7=0.5: `sqrt(A)`. But `sin(A*c2+c3)` ≠ `sin(log(A+1))`. No `A^2`. No match.

**Candidate 51:** `A^c0*c1 + c2 + c3*sin(A*c4+c5) + c6*exp(A*c7)`
- `sin(A*c4+c5)` ≠ `sin(log(A+1))`. No match.

After checking all candidates systematically, none have the combination of `sqrt(A)`, `A^2`, and `sin(log(A+1))` simultaneously achievable.

Let me double-check Candidate 11 and 18 more carefully since they're closest.

**Candidate 11:** `A^2*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*sin(c4*log(c5*|A*c6|+1)+c7)` - missing `sqrt(A)`, only has linear `A`.

**Candidate 18:** Has `A^c2` for sqrt and `A^2`, but `sin(log(exp(...)))` can't match `sin(log(A+1))`.

No candidates match.
